2   package org.freehep.postscript.types;
3   
4   import java.util.HashMap;
5   import java.util.Map;
6   
7   public class UnicodeGlyphList {
8   
9   	private static Map<String, Character> list;
10  
11  	static {
12  		System.err.println("LongList");
13  		list = new HashMap<String, Character>(4500);
14  		// NOTE: method longer than 64K, split into two
15  		initAI();
16  		initJZ();
17  		initZapfDingbats();
18  //		System.err.println("L "+list.size());
19  	}
20  	
21  	private UnicodeGlyphList() {
22  	}
23  	
24  	public static char get(String name) {
25  		Character c = list.get(name);
26  		if (c == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Character '"+name+"' not defined in UnicodeGlyphList");
27  		return c.charValue();
28  	}
